                        "import os\nimport sys\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport logging\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\n\nimport requests\nfrom flask import Flask, request, redirect,  return (\n        f\"https://app.hubspot.com/oauth/authorize?\"\n        f\"client_id={HS_CLIENT_ID}&redirect_uri={HS_REDIRECT_URI}&scope={HS_SCOPE}&response_type=code\"\n    )\n\ndef TOKENS['facebook']['access_token'] = data['access_token']\n    TOKENS['facebook']['expires_in'] = data.get('expires_in', 0)\n    TOKENS['facebook']['obtained_at'] = time.time()\n    logger.info(\"Facebook token obtained.\")\n\ndef exchange_hs_code_for_token(code):\n    url = \"https://api.hubapi.com/oauth/v1/token\"\n    data = {\n        'grant_type': 'authorization_code',\n        'client_id': HS_CLIENT_ID,\n        'client_secret': HS_CLIENT_SECRET,\n        'redirect_uri': HS_REDIRECT_URI,\n        'code': code\n    }\n    resp = requests.post(url, data=data)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    token_data = resp.json()\n    TOKENS['hubspot']['access_token'] = token_data['access_token']\n    TOKENS['hubspot']['refresh_token'] = token_data['refresh_token']\n    TOKENS['hubspot']['expires_in'] = token_data['expires_in']\n    TOKENS['hubspot']['obtained_at'] = time.time()\n    logger.info(\"HubSpot token obtained.\")\n\ndef refresh_hs_token():\n    url = \"https://api.hubapi.com/oauth/v1/token\"\n    data = {\n        'grant_type': 'refresh_token',\n        'client_id': HS_CLIENT_ID,\n        'client_secret': HS_CLIENT_SECRET,\n        'redirect_uri': TOKENS['hubspot']['access_token'] = token_data['access_token']\n    TOKENS['hubspot']['refresh_token'] = token_data['refresh_token']\n    TOKENS['hubspot']['expires_in'] = token_data['expires_in']\n    TOKENS['hubspot']['obtained_at'] = time.time()\n    logger.info(\"HubSpot token refreshed.\")\n\ndef is_token_expired(service):\n    token = TOKENS.get(service, {})\n    if not token:\n        return True\n    expires_in = token.get('expires_in', 0)\n    obtained_at = token.get('obtained_at', 0)\n    return (time.time() - obtained_at) > (expires_in - 60)  # refresh 1 min before expiry\n\n# \"\"\"Create or update a deal in HubSpot for a contact based on ad metrics.\"\"\"\n    url = \"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/deals\"\n    headers = {\n        'Authorization': f\"Bearer OAuth2 code for access token.\"\"\"\n    url = \"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/oauth/access_token\"\n    params = {\n        'client_id': FB_APP_ID,\n        'redirect_uri': FB_REDIRECT_URI,\n        'client_secret': FB_APP_SECRET,\n        'code': code\n    }\n    resp = requests.get(url, params=params)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    return resp.json()\n\ndef exchange_hs_code_for_token(code: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Exchange HubSpot OAuth2 code for access token.\"\"\"\n    url = \"https://api.hubapi.com/oauth/v1/token\"\n    data = {\n        'grant_type': 'authorization_code',\n        'client_id': HS_CLIENT_ID,\n        'client_secret': HS_CLIENT_SECRET,\n        'redirect_uri': HS_REDIRECT_URI,\n        'code': code\n    }\n    headers = {'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'}\n    resp = requests.post(url, data=data, headers=headers)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    return resp.json()\n\n# =======================\n# str, email: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Search for a HubSpot contact by email.\"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/contacts/search\"\n    headers = {'Authorization':   return results[0] if results else None\n\ndef create_or_update_hs_contact(access_token: str, email: str, properties: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Create or update a HubSpot contact.\"\"\"\n    contact = find_hs_contact_by_email(access_token, email)\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {access_token}'}\n    if contact:\n        url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/contacts/{contact['id']}\"\n        resp = requests.patch(url, json={\"properties\": properties}, headers=headers)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        return resp.json()\n    else:\n        url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/contacts\"\n        data = {\"properties\": {\"email\": email, **properties}}\n        resp = requests.post(url, leads = 0\n    for action in ad_metric.get('actions', []):\n        if action.get('action_type') == 'lead':\n            leads += int(action.get('value', 0))\n    mapped['ad_leads'] = leads\n                         "import os\nimport time\nimport threading\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Any\n\nimport requests\nfrom flask import Flask, request, os.getenv('FB_APP_SECRET', 'YOUR_FB_APP_SECRET')\nFB_REDIRECT_URI = os.getenv('FB_REDIRECT_URI', 'http://localhost:5000/fb_callback')\nFB_SCOPE = 'ads_read'\n\nHS_CLIENT_ID = os.getenv('HS_CLIENT_ID', 'contacts deals'\n\nSYNC_INTERVAL_MINUTES = int(os.getenv('SYNC_INTERVAL_MINUTES', '60'))\nFLASK_SECRET_KEY = os.getenv('FLASK_SECRET_KEY', 'supersecretkey')\n\n# =======================\n# OAuth2 URL.\"\"\"\n    return (\n        f\"https://www.facebook.com/v18.0/dialog/oauth?\"\n        f\"client_id={FB_APP_ID}&redirect_uri={FB_REDIRECT_URI}&scope={FB_SCOPE}&response_type=code\"\n    )\n\ndef get_hs_auth_url():\n    \"\"\"Generate HubSpot OAuth2 authorization URL.\"\"\"\n    return (\n        f\"https://app.hubspot.com/oauth/authorize?\"\n        f\"client_id={HS_CLIENT_ID}&redirect_uri={HS_REDIRECT_URI}&scope={HS_SCOPE}&response_type=code\"\n    )\n\ndef exchange_fb_code_for_token(code: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Exchange Facebook OAuth2 code for access token.\"\"\"\n    url = \"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/oauth/access_token\"\n    params = {\n        'client_id': FB_APP_ID,\n        'redirect_uri': FB_REDIRECT_URI,\n        'client_secret': FB_APP_SECRET,\n        'code': code\n    }\n    resp = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=15)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    return resp.json()\n\ndef exchange_hs_code_for_token(code: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Exchange HubSpot OAuth2 code for access token.\"\"\"\n    url = \"https://api.hubapi.com/oauth/v1/token\"\n    data = {\n        'grant_type': 'authorization_code',\n        'client_id': HS_CLIENT_ID,\n        'client_secret': HS_CLIENT_SECRET,\n        'redirect_uri': HS_REDIRECT_URI,\n        'code': code\n    }\n    headers = {'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'}\n    resp = requests.post(url, data=data, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    return resp.json()\n\n# =======================\n# Facebook Marketing API\n# =======================\n\ndef get_fb_ad_accounts(access_token: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n    \"\"\"Fetch Facebook Ad accounts for authenticated user.\"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/me/adaccounts\"\n    params = {'access_token': access_token}\n    resp = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=15)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    return resp.json().get('data', [])\n\ndef get_fb_ad_metrics(access_token: str, account_id: str, since: str, until: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n    \"\"\"Fetch ad metrics for a given account and date range.\"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/{account_id}/insights\"\n    params = {\n        'access_token': access_token,\n        'date_preset': 'custom',\n        'time_range': f'{{\"since\":\"{since}\",\"until\":\"{until}\"}}',\n        'fields': 'campaign_name,adset_name,ad_name,impressions,clicks,spend,actions',\n        'level': 'ad'\n    }\n    resp = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=30)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    return resp.json().get('data', [])\n\n# =======================\n# HubSpot API\n# =======================\n\ndef find_hs_contact_by_email(access_token: str, email: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Find a HubSpot contact by email.\"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/contacts/search\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {access_token}'}\n    data = {\n        \"filterGroups\": [{\n            \"filters\": [{\"propertyName\": \"email\", \"operator\": \"EQ\", \"value\": email}]\n        }],\n        \"properties\": [\"email\", \"firstname\", \"lastname\"]\n    }\n    resp = requests.post(url, json=data, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    results = resp.json().get('results', [])\n    return results[0] if results else None\n\ndef create_or_update_hs_contact(access_token: str, email: str, properties: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Create or update a HubSpot contact.\"\"\"\n    contact = find_hs_contact_by_email(access_token, email)\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {access_token}'}\n    if contact:\n        url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/contacts/{contact['id']}\"\n        resp = requests.patch(url, json={\"properties\": properties}, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        return resp.json()\n    else:\n        url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/contacts\"\n        data = {\"properties\": {\"email\": email, **properties}}\n        resp = requests.post(url, json=data, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        return resp.json()\n\ndef create_or_update_hs_deal(access_token: str, deal_name: str, properties: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Create or update a HubSpot deal by deal name.\"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/deals/search\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {access_token}'}\n    data = {\n        \"filterGroups\": [{\n            \"filters\": [{\"propertyName\": \"dealname\", \"operator\": \"EQ\", \"value\": deal_name}]\n        }],\n        \"properties\": [\"dealname\"]\n    }\n    resp = requests.post(url, return resp.json()\n    else:\n        url = f\"https://api.hubapi.com/crm/v3/objects/deals\"\n        data = {\"properties\": {\"dealname\": deal_name, **properties}}\n        resp = requests.post(url, json=data, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        return resp.json()\n\n# =======================\n# Mapping Logic\n# =======================\n\ndef map_fb_metrics_to_hs(ad_metric: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Map Facebook ad metrics to HubSpot contact/deal properties.\"\"\"\n    mapped = {\n        'ad_campaign_name': ad_metric.get('campaign_name', ''),\n        'adset_name': ad_metric.get('adset_name', ''),\n        'ad_name': ad_metric.get('ad_name', ''),\n        'ad_impressions': int(ad_metric.get('impressions', 0)),\n        'ad_clicks': int(ad_metric.get('clicks', 0)),\n        'ad_spend': float(ad_metric.get('spend', 0.0)),\n    }\n    leads = 0\n    for action in ad_metric.get('actions', []):\n        if action.get('action_type') == 'lead':\n            leads += int(action.get('value', 0))\n    mapped['ad_leads'] = leads\n    return mapped\n\n# =======================\n# Sync Routine\n# =======================\n\nSYNC_HISTORY: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n\ndef sync_facebook_to_hubspot():\n    \"\"\"Pull Facebook ad metrics, map, and push to HubSpot contacts/deals.\"\"\"\n    fb_token = TOKENS['facebook'].get('access_token')\n    hs_token = TOKENS['hubspot'].get('access_token')\n    if not fb_token or not hs_token:\n        print(\"Tokens missing, skipping sync.\")\n        return\n\n    try:\n        ad_accounts = get_fb_ad_accounts(fb_token)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error fetching FB ad accounts: {e}\")\n        return\n\n    # Date range: last 1 day\n    until = datetime.utcnow().date()\n    since = until - timedelta(days=1)\n    since_str = since.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n    until_str = until.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n\n    sync_results = []\n    for account in ad_accounts:\n        account_id = account['id']\n        try:\n            metrics = get_fb_ad_metrics(fb_token, account_id, since_str, until_str)\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Error fetching FB metrics for account {account_id}: {e}\")\n            continue\n\n        for ad in metrics:\n            mapped = map_fb_metrics_to_hs(ad)\n            # For demo, use ad_name as email (real use: map to actual lead email)\n            fake_email = f\"{mapped['ad_name'].replace(' ', '_').lower()}@example.com\"\n            contact_props = {\n                \"firstname\": mapped['ad_campaign_name'],\n                \"lastname\": mapped['adset_name'],\n                \"ad_impressions\": mapped['ad_impressions'],\n                \"ad_clicks\": mapped['ad_clicks'],\n                \"ad_spend\": mapped['ad_spend'],\n                \"ad_leads\": mapped['ad_leads'],\n            }\n            try:\n                contact = create_or_update_hs_contact(hs_token, fake_email, contact_props)\n                deal_props = {\n sync_facebook_to_hubspot()\n        time.sleep(SYNC_INTERVAL_MINUTES * 60)\n\ndef start_auto_sync():\n    \"\"\"Start background thread for auto sync.\"\"\"\n    t =
